		<title>Que Hacer en Momentos de Crisis, Situaciones Altamente Estresantes, y Emergencias</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-primeros-auxilios-psicologicos/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-primeros-auxilios-psicologicos/#respond</comments>

		<pubDate>Wed, 15 Mar 2023 17:57:18 +0000</pubDate>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Review del curso “Primeros Auxilios Psicológicos (PAP)” de la Universitat Autònoma de Barcelona.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-primeros-auxilios-psicologicos/">Que Hacer en Momentos de Crisis, Situaciones Altamente Estresantes, y Emergencias</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<h2><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85741" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></h2>
<h2>Introducción</h2>
<blockquote><p>Es mejor ser un guerrero en el jardín, que ser un jardinero en una guerra &#8211; Dicho Japonés.</p></blockquote>
<p>Si en tu vida diaria y “común”, sucede algún tipo de catástrofe, ¿cómo reaccionarías? ¿Sabrías qué hacer? ¿Sabrías cómo ayudar a las personas involucradas y a tus seres queridos?  Si te gustaría poder responder estas preguntas u obtener más información acerca de cómo reaccionar de manera efectiva y ayudar a otros, <b>“</b><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pap-3224"><b>Primeros Auxilios Psicológicos (PAP)</b></a><b>” </b>de la Universitat Autònoma de Barcelona es perfecto para ti.</p>
<p>Un curso destinado a profesionales, responsables de programas de ayuda a niños y adultos (de forma individual y colectiva), voluntarios en equipos de ayuda y apoyo emocional, y grupos de autoayuda. Sin embargo, el curso también está destinado a la población general y a las personas que buscan obtener más conocimientos e información sobre cómo reaccionar ante situaciones de crisis y estrés, o que, como la frase del principio dice, quieren estar preparados para reaccionar cuando el contexto lo necesite.</p>
<p>Comencemos:</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="Presentación curso Primeros Auxilios Psicológicos de la UAB en Coursera" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/JsgSL9WSS9s?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>Sobre el curso</h2>
<p>Este curso se encuentra dividido en 5 semanas o módulos:</p>
<ul>
<li>        Definición y condiciones de aplicación.</li>
<li>        PAP en niños hasta 12 años.</li>
<li>        PAP en adolescentes y adultos.</li>
<li>        PAP en colectivos especialmente vulnerables.</li>
<li>        Autocuidado del interviniente.</li>
</ul>
<p>Cada uno presenta videos, material de lectura, cuestionarios y ensayos (Peer-graded).</p>
<p>Desde mi punto de vista la información es muy completa y la forma de explicarla y desarrollarla en los videos lo hace más ameno y fácil de entender. Sobre todo, si tenemos en cuenta la naturaleza de esta información, la cual puede ser muy sensible.</p>
<p><b>Modalidad:</b> 100% online.</p>
<p><b>Duración: </b>aproximadamente 15 horas; los limites o “deadlines” son flexibles, por ende, la duración del curso puede depender según la persona.</p>
<p><b>Idioma y subtítulos: </b>español con subtítulos en español e inglés.</p>
<p><b>Certificado:</b> Sí, al finalizar el curso completando los cuestionarios y ensayos, el certificado puede ser compartido en las redes sociales (LinkedIn, por ejemplo).</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="Role Playin Buenas y malas prácticas en la aplicación de los Primeros Auxilios Psicológicos" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/WOFeXocyUow?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>Mi experiencia</h2>
<p>Desde la separación y clasificación de cómo accionar con personas de diferentes edades y contextos, hasta el último módulo donde se habla de algo no tan conocido o tomado en cuenta por el público en general: la salud mental del interviniente, el curso explica de forma directa y muy práctica.</p>
<p>Este curso nos brinda herramientas simples pero muy útiles y necesarias: nos enseña a como dirigirnos a este tipo de personas, que preguntas hacerles, y a tratarlos con respeto y dignidad.</p>
<p>Mi interés por este curso nace por mi pasión y carrera; la psicología. Como psicólogos debemos ser capaces de identificar cuando el paciente presenta rasgos de estrés y/o crisis (Estrés Post Traumático, por ejemplo) y cómo tratarlo; esto puede ser muy peligroso, debido a que debemos calmarlo y no alarmarlo ni confundirlo más de lo que está.</p>
<p>Y, sobre todo, si el día de mañana uno de mis pacientes son profesionales que se encargan de asistir personas en situaciones de crisis, ahora conozco su realidad, sus problemas, puedo empatizar con todo el estrés debido a la gran responsabilidad que tienen y que muchas veces puede ser muy injusta en ellos.</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="Introducción al 5º módulo del curso MOOC sobre Primeros Auxilios Psicológicos de la UAB en Coursera" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/OG8Ei2ypRxE?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>Conclusión</h2>
<p>No queda mucho que decir, en mi opinión, este es un curso el cual uno no debe estar involucrado con profesiones relacionadas a la salud exclusivamente, este es un curso el cual cada persona puede aprender algo nuevo e inclusive, ser el héroe cuando la situación lo amerite.</p>
<p>Espero que este artículo le haya servido y que lo empuje a aprender e investigar más sobre los primeros auxilios psicológicos.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85743" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap.png" alt="" width="480" height="370" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap.png 480w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap-300x231.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /></p>

]]></content:encoded>

		<item>
		<title>What to do in Moments of Crisis, Highly Stressful Situations, and Emergencies</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-psychological-first-aid/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-psychological-first-aid/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Agustin Cardone]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Wed, 15 Mar 2023 17:56:59 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Reviews]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=85740</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>Review of the course "Psychological First Aid (PFA)" from Universitat Autònoma de Barcelona.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-psychological-first-aid/">What to do in Moments of Crisis, Highly Stressful Situations, and Emergencies</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<h2><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85741" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Primeros-Auxilios-Psicologicos-PAP-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></h2>
<h2>Introduction</h2>
<blockquote><p>It is better to be a warrior in the garden, than to be a gardener in a war &#8211; Japanese saying.</p></blockquote>
<p>If in your daily and &#8220;common&#8221; life, some kind of catastrophe happens, how would you react? Would you know what to do? Would you know how to help the people involved and your loved ones? If you would like to be able to answer these questions or obtain more information about how to react effectively and help others, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pap-3224">Psychological First Aid (PFA)</a> from <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/uab">Universitat Autònoma de Barcelona</a> is perfect for you.</p>
<p>Although this is a course for professionals responsible for aid programs for children and adults (individually and collectively), it’s also useful for volunteers, self-help groups and the general population. People who seek more knowledge on how to react to crises, handle stressful situations, or as the sentence at the beginning says, want to be prepared to react when the context requires it.</p>
<p>Let&#8217;s begin:</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="Psychological First Aid - Singapore Red Cross" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/sQGXSSs6Cpo?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>About the course</h2>
<p>This course is divided into 5 weeks or modules:</p>
<ul>
<li>        Definition and application conditions.</li>
<li>        PFA in children up to 12 years.</li>
<li>        PFA in adolescents and adults.</li>
<li>        PFA in especially vulnerable groups.</li>
<li>        Self-care of the intervener.</li>
</ul>
<p>Each features videos, reading material, quizzes, and essays (Peer-graded).</p>
<p>From my point of view, the information is very complete and the way it is explained and developed in the videos makes it more enjoyable and easier to understand. Above all, the nature of this information can be very sensitive.</p>
<p><b>Modality:</b> 100% online.</p>
<p><b>Duration: </b>about 15 hours; the limits or &#8220;deadlines&#8221; are flexible, therefore, the duration of the course may depend on the person.</p>
<p><b>Language: </b>course in Spanish with Spanish and English subtitles.</p>
<p><b>Certificate:</b> Yes, at the end of the course by completing the questionnaires and essays. The certificate can be shared on social networks (LinkedIn, for example).</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="How to give psychological first aid" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/IOUM_208sJA?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>My experience</h2>
<p>This course covers the separation and classification of how to act with people of different ages and contexts. The last module explains the mental health of the intervener in a direct and very practical way. This is something not so well known or taken into account by the general public.</p>
<p>The course provides us with simple but very useful and necessary tools: It teaches us how to address different types of people, what questions to ask them and to treat them with respect and dignity.</p>
<p>My interest in this course stems from my passion and career; psychology. As psychologists we must be able to identify when the patient presents traits of stress and/or crisis (Post Traumatic Stress, for example) and how to treat it; This can be very dangerous because we must calm the patient down and not alarm or confuse them more.</p>
<p>And, above all, if tomorrow one of my patients is a professional who is in charge of assisting people in crises, now I know their reality, their problems, I can empathize with all the stress due to the great responsibility they have and acknowledge that it can be very unfair on them.</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="How To Support Someone Who Is Experiencing Mental Ill-Health | The ALGEE Model | 3 Minute Explainer" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/FXnPeKLrD-w?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<h2>Conclusion</h2>
<p>There is not much left to say, in my opinion, this is a course in which one should not be involved with professions related to health exclusively, this is a course in which each person can learn something new and even be the hero when the situation deserves it.</p>
<p>I hope this article has helped you and that it encourages you to learn and investigate more about psychological first aid.</p>
<figure id="attachment_85743" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85743" style="width: 480px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85743" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap.png" alt="" width="480" height="370" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap.png 480w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/certificate-agustin-pap-300x231.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85743" class="wp-caption-text">My certificate of completion.</figcaption></figure>

]]></content:encoded>

With the right skills and knowledge, you can unlock the power of big data and make a real impact in your career. So, buckle up, grab a cup of coffee, and let’s start exploring Data Science together! What are you waiting for? Let’s get started!</p>

<h2>What is Data Science?</h2>
<p>Data science is a field that utilizes scientific induction to extract general principles from specific observations. With the <a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/bernardmarr/2018/05/21/how-much-data-do-we-create-every-day-the-mind-blowing-stats-everyone-should-read/?sh=1887a60060ba" target="_blank" rel="noopener">vast amount of data</a> generated daily in the digital age, it would be impossible for humans to sift through them all to discover trends. This is where data scientists come in, offloading the difficult computational work to machines through machine learning or deep learning.</p>
<p>However, data scientists are needed to ensure that the data fed to the machines is clean and the right machine is chosen, and to communicate the findings to those who may not be as technically inclined. This challenging and rewarding field has been <a href="https://business.linkedin.com/content/dam/me/business/en-us/talent-solutions/emerging-jobs-report/Emerging_Jobs_Report_U.S._FINAL.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">gaining popularity</a>, being hailed as the <a href="https://hbr.org/2012/10/data-scientist-the-sexiest-job-of-the-21st-century" target="_blank" rel="noopener">sexiest job of the 21st century</a> by Harvard and paying a median salary of <a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/data-scientist-salary-SRCH_KO0,14.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener">$120k per year</a> in the United States.</p>
<p>Data analytics, a subset of data science, has also been gaining traction, and Python and R are the most popular programming languages used in the field. With data galore and new technologies emerging every day, data science is set to become an increasingly important and exciting field for years to come.</p>
<h2>My Experience with Data Science</h2>
<p>I built this ranking in collaboration with my friend and colleague<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@manoel" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> @manoel</a>.</p>
<p>We both come from computer science backgrounds and are prolific online learners, having completed about 45 MOOCs between us. Additionally, Manoel has an<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/open-university-insiders-perspective/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> online bachelor’s in computer science</a>, while I am currently completing my foundation in computer science. In fact, data science is the primary reason I’m interested in CS!</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2>Course Ranking Methodology</h2>
<p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> 100K online courses</a> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/data-science" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2,900+ Data Science courses</a> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> learner</a>.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, affordability, release date, ratings and enrollments.</li>
</ol>
<p>After going through this process — combining Class Central data, our experience as lifelong learners, and a lot of editing — we arrived at our final ranking. So far, we’ve spent more than 21 hours building this ranking, and we intend to continue updating it in the future.</p>
<p>One note about this ranking. Although data science is typically considered a superset of data analytics, data analytics has been getting a lot of traction in its own right, so I’ve also included picks that explicitly focus on data analytics in this ranking. We’ve also made sure to include Python and R as they are the most popular programming languages used for data science.</p>
<h2>Course Ranking Statistics</h2>
<p>Here are some aggregate stats about the ranking:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">The number of enrollments for each course combines to a total of 6.4 million enrollments, with the highest enrolled course having 1.6 million enrollments.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Seven of the courses are free or free-to-audit, while three courses are paid.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Seven courses are beginner level, with the rest at an intermediate level.</li>
<li aria-level="1">This course has a diverse list of 6 providers, with the most-represented provider being Coursera.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Three of the courses in this ranking uses Python, two uses R, and the rest does not involve coding.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Around 348k people are following <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/data-science" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Data Science Courses on Class Central</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p>Without further ado, let’s get to the top picks.</p>
<h2 id="first">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-introduction-to-computational-thinking-and-data-science-1779" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Computational Thinking and Data Science (Massachusetts Institute of Technology)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78980 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-11.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-11.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-11-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-11-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My #1 pick for the best data science course is for <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-introduction-to-computational-thinking-and-data-science-1779" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Computational Thinking and Data Science</a>, offered by the Massachusetts Institute of Technology on edX.</p>
<p>This <b>free-to-audit</b> course is designed to teach you with a wide variety of concepts and methods to excel in computational thinking and data science, and does so very rigorously, as you’d expect from an MIT course. This course has by far the highest workload in the ranking!</p>
<p>This course is a continuation of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-introduction-to-computer-science-and-programming-using-python-1341" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Computer Science and Programming Using Python</a>, although if you have prior Python programming experience and some knowledge of algorithms and complexity, you should be ready to take this course. If you need, check out one of the courses in my <a href="https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/best-python-courses" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Python ranking</a>.</p>
<p>Be aware that since this course is a one-to-one reflection of what students at MIT learn and do on campus, you may find some of the course material and assignments challenging. Remember, challenge brings effort, and effort brings success!</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The major topics discussed in this course are optimization problems, stochastic thinking, modeling aspects of the world, and advanced features and libraries of Python.</span></p>
<p>The course starts with an introduction to optimization models, which are mathematical models designed to identify the best possible solution for a problem under a set of constraints. Problems are typically formulated as a function with a specific goal, such as maximizing or minimizing the results of the function. For example,  an optimization model could be used to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Travelling_salesman_problem" target="_blank" rel="noopener">find the shortest distance from one city to another</a>. However, solving for multiple parameters can be challenging and time-consuming. Therefore, the course will cover various techniques and algorithms used to efficiently solve optimization problems.</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introducing efficient algorithms. You’ll gain knowledge of the most common and useful algorithms and models used in computer science — to name a few: greedy algorithms, breadth-first search, and depth-first search. You’ll use these to tackle optimization problems, like the </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knapsack_problem" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">knapsack problem</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, curve fitting on graphs, and clustering.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Next, the course explores stochastic thinking — that is, thinking in terms of probabilities. Randomness is an incredibly powerful tool for building computations that model the world. You’ll use randomness to simulate solutions to problems, like </span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Birthday_problem" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">what’s the probability that two people in a group share the same birthday</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, or even solve problems that do not involve randomness, like estimating the area under a curve.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">To analyze the answers to the problems you’ve simulated, the course covers a couple of important statistical techniques. These include plotting probability density functions with PyLab and their types of distribution, confidence intervals, sampling and standard error, and much more.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course also introduces machine learning. You’ll distinguish between supervised and unsupervised learning, and deep dive into the theory behind machine learning applications, like linear regression and clustering. While we’re on the subject, if you’re interested in machine learning, you may want to </span><a href="https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/best-machine-learning-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">have a look at this ranking</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<blockquote><p><span style="font-weight: 400;">There are three kinds of lies: lies, damned lies, and statistics.</span></p></blockquote>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The final section of the course ends by discussing the limitations and pitfalls of statistics, and then explaining how to avoid some of the common statistical </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">sins</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> used to mislead people.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is 9 weeks long, with an expected 14 to 16 hours of study time each week. You’ll learn through video lectures and you’ll spend time applying what you’ve been taught in the problem sets provided.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Regarding assessments, the problem sets and exams can be taken for free, although you’ll need to be a verified learner to earn a certificate.</span></p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course has 8.3k bookmarks on Class Central.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is based on the book </span><a href="https://mitpress.mit.edu/books/introduction-computation-and-programming-using-python-second-edition" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introduction to Computation and Programming Using Python, Second Edition</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It’s the second and last course of the edX XSeries Program, </span><a href="https://www.edx.org/xseries/mitx-computational-thinking-using-python" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Computational Thinking using Python</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prof. Eric Grimson, the lead course instructor, has a </span><a href="https://scholar.google.com/citations?user=zZ0-4SUAAAAJ&amp;hl=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">79 h-index on Google Scholar</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> — if you’re wondering, yes, that’s a lot!</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-introduction-to-computational-thinking-and-data-science-1779" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">more information about the course and how to enroll here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<h2 id="second">2. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-data-35107" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Foundations: Data, Data, Everywhere (Google)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78973 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-7.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-7.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-7-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-7-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My second pick for the best data science course is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-data-35107" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Foundations: Data, Data, Everywhere</a>, offered by Google on Coursera. If you’re looking for a program that’ll prepare you for a data analytics career, this <b>free-to-audit</b> course might be what you need because it’s very hands-on and job-oriented.</p>
<p>Taught by Google’s own data analysts, this course provides you with the skills and mindset necessary to become a successful junior data analyst. You’ll understand what it means to be a data analyst and learn what tools and processes data analysts use in their day-to-day workflow.</p>
<p>You won’t need any prior experience in order to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course covers the roles and responsibilities of a junior data analyst, how businesses transform data into actionable insights, spreadsheet basics, database and query basics, and data visualization basics.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course begins with an introduction to data and data analytics. Data is a collection of raw information, while data analysis is the process of piecing together data to draw conclusions, form predictions, and make decisions. You’ll learn the role data analysts play in informing smarter business decisions.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The next section hammers down five essential skills of data analysts, and five key aspects of analytical thinking. You&#8217;ll see how having these abilities turns you into a better data-driven decision-maker.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Afterwards, you’ll explore the six stages of the data life cycle, like capturing, analyzing, and destroying data. With this knowledge, you’ll understand how to approach the data analysis process, which consists of six phases. Yes, there are a lot of stages to take into account, but remember that following these phases ensures that you don’t accidentally overlook an important matter — say sanitizing or standardizing your data!</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll open up and peek into the data analyst’s toolbox. The course will discuss two ways we can store data: in spreadsheets like Microsoft Excel or Google Sheets; or in databases that we can interact with using query languages like SQL. You’ll understand when to use one over the other. Additionally, the course will cover how to visualize data patterns and trends with tools like Tableau, Looker, and R.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lastly, you’ll look into the various kinds of job opportunities available for data analysts, the best practices in the job search, and what companies expect from your work. The course ends with a reminder of the importance of fairness and avoiding bias when analyzing data for business tasks.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is 5 weeks long with an average workload of 4 hours per week. The primary medium of instruction is video lectures and reading materials, both of which are excellent in terms of production quality.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Regarding assessments, there’ll be 5 weekly challenges plus a final course challenge that you’ll have to complete to earn a grade if you’re paying for the certificate. Not only that, the course provides multiple short quizzes and flashcards that you can use to revise what you’ve learned.</span></p>

It helps prepare you for applying to entry-level data analyst jobs. </span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The professional certificate uses the R programming language. No Python here!</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">As one of the largest companies in the world when it comes to data collection and storage, Google employs a huge number of data scientists, making them an excellent source for learning data science.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-data-35107" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">more information about the course and how to enroll here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<h2 id="third">3. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-data-science-r-basics-9253" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Data Science: R Basics (Harvard University)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78972 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-8.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-8.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-8-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-8-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My third pick for the best data science course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-data-science-r-basics-9253" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Data Science: R Basics</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by Harvard University on edX. </span></p>
<p>What sets this <b>free-to-audit</b> course apart from others is its unique pedagogy. Through a case study focusing on crime in the United States, you’ll analyze and use a dataset to answer questions like ‘What is the smallest state?’,  ‘What is the most dangerous state?’, and ‘What is the average murder rate in the entirety of the US?’ — without googling of course!</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Although no programming experience is required, the course assumes you are comfortable with basic math and algebra.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is split into four sections: R Basics, Vectors and Sorting, Wrangling and Visualizing Data, and Programming Basics.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Beginning with the fundamentals of R and RStudio, you’ll understand what makes R a popular language for data analysis. You’ll study what objects are, how to define and perform basic arithmetic and logical operations with them. The course covers a couple of important pre-defined functions in R. You’ll also be able to distinguish between the various data types in R (3 and ‘3’ are two different things!).</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Next, you’ll come across another important feature of R — vectors. Vectors are powerful as they form the building blocks of big datasets. You’ll create vectors and use them to build lists of cities or sequences of numbers which you can then sort or sum. The course guides you on the basics of vector arithmetics, like how to add two vectors together or what it means to scale a vector. Additionally, you’ll use indexing and subsetting methods to find the most dangerous state in America.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lastly, you’ll be taught the basics of plotting in R, to help communicate your insights to a wider audience. You’ll learn four different kinds of plots you can use to visualize patterns and trends in the data: line plot, histogram, boxplot, and heatmap.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is 8 weeks long, with each week taking 1 to 2 hours to complete. The course contains a series of many video lectures and reading materials.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Regarding assessments, some of the exercises in the course involve writing code and submitting it directly through </span><a href="https://www.datacamp.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">DataCamp’s</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> browser-based programming environment, although major assessments must be completed using RStudio.</span></p>

<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Data Science: R Basics</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> has 7.8k bookmarks on Class Central.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">It is the first course out of nine from Harvard’s intensive </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-data-science-18421" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Data Science Professional Certificate</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Professional Certificates comes with </span><a href="https://rafalab.github.io/dsbook/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">a companion book</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> written by Rafael Irizarry, the course instructor.</span></li>

If you enjoy DataCamp, you may want to check our <a href="#fifth" target="_blank" rel="noopener">fifth pick below</a>.</span></li>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-data-science-r-basics-9253" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">more information about the course and how to enroll here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<h2 id="fourth">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-python-for-data-science-course-for-beginners-learn-python-pandas-numpy-matplotlib-66061" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Python for Data Science &#8211; Course for Beginners (Learn Python, Pandas, NumPy, Matplotlib)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78976 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-4.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-4.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-4-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-4-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you want to learn data science with Python but have no programming experience, this course is for you.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This beginner-friendly, <b>free</b> course on freeCodeCamp’s YouTube channel will guide you from the ground up to help you acquire the fundamentals of both Python and data science. The course not only covers Python and data science from a conceptual standpoint, it also covers the tools and libraries data scientists use, like Anaconda, NumPy, Pandas, and Matplotlib, so you get plenty of practical experience as well.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course covers four main topics: Problem Solving, Python’s strength, Python fundamentals, and Data Science.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course starts off with a tutorial on problem solving with programming, the most essential skill any programmer should have. You’ll learn how to approach complex problems and break them down into simpler parts, along with simple algorithms. You’ll then install and run Python with Anaconda, a popular distribution of Python used for data science.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Once you have set up your </span><a href="https://jupyter.org/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Jupyter Notebook</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> coding environment, you’ll move on to the basics of Python programming. This includes learning about variables and operators, booleans and comparisons, control flow and functions, and much much more. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course then instructs you on some more advanced Python topics, like importing and using Python modules, modifying and parsing text, as well as key data structures like lists, tuples, sets and dictionaries, and when to use one over the other. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">All of these combined will make you an excellent Python programmer capable of writing small programs. But that is not all the course will teach you.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll be introduced to three of the most popular Python libraries used in data science. Starting with NumPy, you’ll write fast and efficient code with NumPy arrays that are 5–100 times faster than regular Python lists. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Afterwards you’ll move on to NumPy’s big brother, Pandas. Pandas is used to represent and compute rows and columns of data (put differently tables) which you’ll be dealing with a lot of as a data scientist. Finally, you’ll learn about Matplotlib, a highly-configurable data visualization library that allows you to plot and reveal the patterns hiding within data.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is 12 hours long and presented in a lecture-and-slide-s format, with frequent coding demonstrations. You are expected to code along with the instructor in order to apply and retain the concepts taught.</span></p>

<h2 id="fifth">5. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/datacamp-data-science-for-everyone-24379" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Understanding Data Science (Datacamp)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78975 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-5.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-5.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-5-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-5-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Similar to <a href="#second" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Google’s Foundations: Data, Data, Everywhere</a> but much shorter, DataCamp’s </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/datacamp-data-science-for-everyone-24379" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Understanding Data Science</i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> teaches data science with no coding involved. If you’re not sure about what data science actually is and what its applications are, this course will enlighten you.</span></p>
<p><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Data Science for Everyone</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> introduces you to the world of data science, the different roles and responsibilities a data scientist may have, as well as the kind of work data scientists do as part of their career.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You do not need any prior experience in order to take this course.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Data science simply defined is the set of methodologies for taking in data at scale and using them to draw meaningful conclusions. You’ll uncover the first four steps of the data science workflow: data collection &amp; storage, data preparation, exploration &amp; visualization, and experimentation &amp; prediction. The course then describes the four common jobs of data science — data engineer, data analyst, data scientist, and machine learning scientist — and where they fit in the data science workflow. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course unpacks the first step of the data science workflow: data collection &amp; storage. You’ll learn where data scientists extract their data from, what data looks like and how to efficiently store them, and how a data pipeline can automate the process.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Next, you’ll learn about step two and three of the workflow: data preparation, exploration and visualization. Data preparation is the most important part of the data science workflow. Data scientists spend 80% of their time sanitizing their data because of Garbage In, Garbage Out principle — if you give a model garbage, then the predictions you get will be garbage. You’ll learn how to explore your dataset and deal with common problems such as missing values and outliers. Once you have cleaned up your data, you’ll learn about the common tools data scientists use to create beautiful visualizations.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Finally, you’ll learn about the experimentation and prediction step of the data science workflow. The course focuses on a variety of statistical techniques like A/B testing, testing for statistical significance, and time series forecasting. The course ends with a section on the differences between supervised and unsupervised machine learning and when to use them.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course in its entirety is 2 hours long and consists of 4 parts, with each section containing video lectures and exercises. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">One thing I like about DataCamp is that the course gives you many opportunities to retain what you’ve learned from the video material through interactive exercises.</span></p>

<h2 id="sixth">6. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/data-science-crash-course-4392" target="_blank" rel="noopener">A Crash Course in Data Science (Johns Hopkins University)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78974 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-6.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-6.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-6-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-6-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/data-science-crash-course-4392" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>A Crash Course in Data Science</i></a> by John Hopkins University is a short but intensive overview of data science — no coding involved. What makes it different from the previous listing is that it&#8217;s geared towards non-technical people who’ll manage and/or work with data scientists.</p>
<p>The goal of this <b>free-to-audit</b> course is to get you up to speed as fast as possible so that you can get to work reaping the benefits of practical data science. The course is taught from a high-level perspective, hence it will only cover the essentials without getting into the technical aspects.</p>
<p>There are no prerequisites required prior to taking this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course starts off by emphasizing the </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">science</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in data science. Science begins with the scientific hypothesis and then tries to confirm its validity by performing experiments, with the ultimate goal of  achieving useful results. Likewise, data science should start with a series of questions. What is the question you&#8217;re trying to answer with data? Do you have the data to actually answer that question? How would the answer be useful?</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll learn how statistics, machine learning, and software engineering play a huge role in data science. For example, what is cross validation? What&#8217;s the difference between supervised and unsupervised learning? What programming languages do data scientists use? You’ll understand these key terms and tools so that you can communicate effectively with data scientists.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Afterwards, you’ll explore the structure of a data science project.  You’ll study the stages of the data science workflow and how they contribute to the overall result, like exploratory data analysis and formal modeling. Lastly, you’ll learn how data scientists communicate their insights to others, and how to determine if a data science project is successful.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is 1 week long with 7 to 8 hours of material. It supplies you with various video and reading materials to learn from, along with several assignments to consolidate your learning. However, you can only access the assignments if you have paid for the certification or the whole specialization.</span></p>

<h2 id="seventh">7. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/procmin-2445" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Process Mining: Data Science in Action (Eindhoven University of Technology)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78979 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-1.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>This <b>free-to-audit</b> course, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/procmin-2445" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i>Process Mining: Data science in Action</i></a> is quite different from the other courses in this ranking in terms of contents. For starters, this course won’t teach you coding. What it does teach you is the key theoretical tools and analytical skills needed to perform process mining — not “just” data mining, we are higher in the ladder of abstraction here, and we’re entering specialized territory.</p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course asserts that processes should be considered first-class citizens, to the same extent as data, and therefore, that they should be put through the same scrutiny.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course provides easy-to-use software, real-life data sets, and practical skills for you to directly apply the theory in a variety of application domains.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">More on process mining: process mining is a technique used to analyze and track processes. Its goal is to help organizations turn event data into actionable insight. Example applications include: analyzing treatment processes in hospitals, understanding the browsing behavior of customers using booking sites, analyzing failures of a baggage handling system, and improving the user interface of an X-ray machine.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">After taking this course, you’ll be able to run process mining projects and have a good understanding of the Business Process Intelligence field. You’ll also benefit from practical data science knowledge that can be applied directly to analyze and improve processes in a variety of domains. So this course has well defined scope within data science that may be suitable for learners that already have a background in the field and would like to explore an additional facet.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course assumes a basic understanding of logic, sets, and statistics at the undergraduate level prior to taking this course.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course starts with an overview of approaches and technologies that use event data to support decision making and business process (re)design. </span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The first type of process mining is discovery. A discovery technique takes an event log and produces a process model without using any a-priori information. You’ll be given an example of an algorithm taking an event log to produce a process model  explaining the behavior recorded in the log. The course then shows you other ways of discovering a process model from event data.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The second type of process mining is conformance. Here, an existing process model is compared with an event log of the same process. You’ll learn how to perform conformance checking to determine if reality, as recorded in the log, conforms to the model and vice versa.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lastly, you’ll find how process mining can be applied on running processes, which is the third type of process mining called enhancement. The idea is to extend or improve an existing process model using information about the actual process recorded in some event log. The course also addresses how to get the right event data, process mining software, and how to get from data to results.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course spans 6 weeks, with each week taking 3 to 6 hours to complete. Every module consists of a series of short lecture videos of 8–15 minutes each, with handouts for each video lecture available to be downloaded.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Regarding assessments, there will be weekly quizzes to test your understanding of the lecture videos, and a final exam. There’s also an optional peer assignment in which you apply the tools and techniques on real data and make a short report.</span></p>

<h2 id="eighth">8. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/datasciencemathskills-7745" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Data Science Math Skills (Duke University)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78978 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-2.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Data science courses contain math — there’s no avoiding that!</p>
<p>The aim of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/datasciencemathskills-7745" target="_blank" rel="noopener">this free-to-audit course</a> is to teach fledgling data scientists the core mathematical concepts data science is built upon, introducing unfamiliar ideas and math symbols one at a time. By the end of this course, you’ll be ready to tackle almost any in-depth data science course out there.</p>
<p>To take this course, you’ll only need basic math skills. No algebra or pre-calculus needed.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Beginning with basic set theory, you’ll learn about unions, intersections, and cardinality, and how to represent them with Venn diagrams. A real-world application of set theory is in medical testing, where false positives and false negatives exist. Then, you’ll study the properties of the real number line and how to represent inequalities with interval notation. The course then teaches you how to represent sums with the Sigma notation.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The next part of the course touches on functions and graphs. The Cartesian plane is the most common way to plot data. You’ll learn how to find the equation of a line given two points. After that, you’ll approach a function as an input-output machine, and see how to graph on the Cartesian plane, as well as its inverse.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll be given a gentle introduction to calculus. You’ll learn about the concept of instantaneous rate of change and how it relates to finding a tangent line to a curve, as well as its applications in the real-world problem of optimization. You’ll learn about continuous growth, and the special constant known as Euler’s number. You’ll also explore exponents, logarithms, and the natural log function.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course ends with probability theory — the study of uncertain but predictable outcomes — and its vocabulary and notation. You’ll study permutations and combinations which are the ways in which a set of things can be arranged, leading to the well-known Binomial and Bayes theorems. You’ll see how these theorems are able to predict the probability of a process given data that we have observed.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is 4 weeks long with an estimated 13 hours worth of material. You’ll primarily learn through video lectures and supplemental readings, and of course, quizzes to test your knowledge.</span></p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://memp.pratt.duke.edu/faculty-staff/louis-egger" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Daniel Egger</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, the course co-instructor, has more than seventeen years of experience creating new software products and services.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Meanwhile, </span><a href="https://www.paulbendich.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Paul Bendich</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> directs the Data+ program which explores </span><a href="https://bigdata.duke.edu/data" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">new data-driven approaches to interdisciplinary challenges</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/datasciencemathskills-7745" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">more information about the course and how to enroll here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<h2 id="nineth">9. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-python-for-machine-learning-data-science-ma-25709" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2022 Python for Machine Learning &amp; Data Science Masterclass (Udemy)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78977 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-3.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-3.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-3-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-3-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you are already familiar with Python programming and want to start straight away with practical data science (especially machine learning), <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udemy-python-for-machine-learning-data-science-ma-25709" target="_blank" rel="noopener">this course is for you</a>. This Udemy course is the most comprehensive all-in-one package in this ranking — at least, in terms of breadth; in terms of workload, <a href="#first" target="_blank" rel="noopener">our first pick remains the king</a>.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">What I like the most about this course is that it goes through the history, theory and intuition behind each machine learning algorithm before you start applying it, unlike some courses out there. This unfortunately (or fortunately for nerds like us) means the course will expose you to math and statistics, but nothing too overwhelming. Knowing some highschool mathematics and statistics should be enough to be comfortable taking this course.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers NumPy, Pandas, Seaborn, Matplotlib, Plotly, Scikit-Learn, and supervised and unsupervised machine learning.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">After setting up your Anaconda environment (a distribution of Python popular with data scientists) and a quick crash course on Python, the course begins with an introduction to NumPy and Pandas. These two libraries are arguably the backbone of Python data science as they speed up the data-centric programming process greatly. The power of modifying tables of huge datasets will be in your hands now.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Then, you’ll want to visualize whatever data you have. The course shows you two plotting libraries you’ll most often use in your data science career: Matplotlib, complex but highly configurable, and Seaborn, simple but less configurable. You’ll then learn the different kinds of plots these libraries have to offer, like the line plot, scatter plot, box plot, bar plot, and a whole bunch more. You’ll learn the strengths and weaknesses of each of these plots and when to use them.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Next, you’ll move on to the appetizing core of the course — machine learning. After cleaning and sanitizing your dataset, you’ll begin by learning the different types of machine learning models like supervised or unsupervised, and regression and classification. You’ll also discuss the limitations of machine learning —  you’ll need to keep these in mind to avoid biased and unfair predictions.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll start with the simplest of supervised machine learning models — linear regression. The course builds on and expands on linear regression by bringing in regularization, lasso regression, ridge regression and Elastic Net. Then, the course moves to supervised classification models, like Support Vector Machines, Decision Trees and Random Forests. A small section on Natural Language Processing is included.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">We then switch gears to unsupervised machine learning models. K-Nearest Neighbors, K-Means Clustering, DBSCAN, and Principal Component Analysis will be some of the popular models that you’ll discover. Throughout your studies, you’ll learn the history and intuition behind each and every model — a full course meal!</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lastly, you’ll learn how to deploy your model to the web as an API, along with a few other considerations, like how often you should retrain and revisit your model and so on.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is split up into 26 different sections, with a grand total of 44 hours of lecture material. The course will provide you with the Jupyter notebooks used in the video demonstrations, which are excellent notes to refer to.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">There are many exercises that you’ll have to complete that’ll help strengthen your knowledge, and don’t worry — there are solutions walkthrough. On top of that, there are two capstone projects that you’ll complete to test your ability to work independently as a data scientist.</span></p>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The courses he teaches range from basic Python programming to web development to deep learning.</span></li>

It’s an especially good read for beginners.</span></li>

<h2 id="tenth">10. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-r-data-science-51183" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Data Science with R (Pluralsight)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-78971 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-9.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-9.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-9-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Banner-9-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/pluralsight-r-data-science-51183" target="_blank" rel="noopener">This course</a> from Pluralsight aims to teach data science — the act of transforming data into actionable insights — using the R programming language. By the end of this course, you&#8217;ll have the skills necessary to use R to perform data analysis and deploy your own web-based interactive machine learning models.</p>
<p>There are no prerequisites for this course, although having some basic knowledge of programming and statistics would be helpful.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course covers three main topics: data science and R, data analysis, and machine learning.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course begins with an introduction to data science with the R programming language. You’ll learn what features of R make it an awesome tool for data analytics, and how you can use R to create actionable insight from data.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Afterwards, you’ll understand how and why you should clean up your data before analyzing it. You’ll learn how to interpret descriptive statistics like mean and median, visualize data to make it easy for your audience to understand the trends and patterns involved, and build statistical models to form simple predictions with your data.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lastly, you’ll deal with big data — datasets that are too large and complex to effectively process with traditional statistical models and methods. This type of dataset is an ideal use case for machine learning. You’ll understand how machine learning algorithms work in order to make predictions with big data. Finally, you’ll deploy your interactive machine learning application on the web.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course consists of 10 sections containing video lectures, demonstrations of the lecture, and summaries. All in all, the course has around 2.5 hours of learning materials.</span></p>

<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">What is User Experience (UX)?</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">User experience (or UX) refers to how people interact with a product. In the digital design world, it encompasses everything that affects a user’s interaction with a digital product such as its value, function, usability and overall impression.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The term “user experience” was coined by Don Norman in the 1990s and refers to all aspects of the end-user’s interaction with a company, its services, and its products. UX is about what users both think and feel, and it depends on the context in which the product is used. However, a user’s experience with a product may change over time, which means the ongoing evaluation and improvement is necessary.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience (UX) vs. User Interface (UI)</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">User experience (UX) is different from user interface (UI). While UI focuses on the visual and interactive elements of a product, UX encompasses the overall experience a user has with a product, including how easy it is to use, how it makes the user feel, and whether it provides value to the user. UI is just one component of UX, and an effective UX design involves much more than just creating an attractive interface.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Why are User Experience Skills Important?</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX skills are essential because they help businesses create products that users find valuable and enjoyable to use. When a product is well-designed with a good user experience, it can help businesses retain customers, increase sales, and build a positive brand reputation. Additionally, as more and more business is conducted online, having strong UX skills can give designers and developers a competitive edge in the job market.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The future of UX designers is bright, as the demand for user experience skills is constantly increasing. With the world becoming more digital, companies are increasingly realizing the importance of creating positive user experiences for their products and services. The job market for UX designers is expected to grow 14% from 2019 to 2029, which is much faster than the average for all occupations.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">As for salaries, the average pay for UX designers varies greatly depending on location and experience level. According to </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/ux-designer-salary-SRCH_KO0,11.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Glassdoor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, the average salary for UX designers in the United States is around $97,000 per year. In the </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/united-kingdom-ux-designer-salary-SRCH_IL.0,14_IN2_KO15,26.htm?clickSource=careerNav" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">United Kingdom</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, the average salary is around £53,000 per year. In </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.com/Salaries/sydney-user-experience-designer-salary-SRCH_IL.0,6_IM962_KO7,31.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Australia</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, the average salary is around AU$100,000 per year, and in </span><a href="https://www.glassdoor.co.in/Salaries/user-experience-designer-salary-SRCH_KO0,24.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">India</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, it is around INR 8 lakh per year. These are just averages, and salaries can range from around $50,000 to over $150,000 depending on experience, location, and other factors.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Methodology</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in previous rankings (</span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). It involves a three-step process:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">100K online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/ux" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">440+ User Experience courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">learner</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, release date, affordability, ratings and enrollments.</span></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The end result is a unique selection of courses that combines a decade of Class Central data and my own experience as an online learner to try to get the best of both worlds. So far, I’ve spent more than 12 hours building this list, and I’ll continue to update it.</span></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Course Ranking Statistics</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here are some statistics regarding this course ranking:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Combined, these courses have accrued over </span><b>1M</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> enrollments.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">9 courses are </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> or </span><b>free-to-audit</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 1 course is </span><b>paid</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The most-represented course provider in the ranking is </span><b>Coursera</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">, with 7 courses.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">All 10 courses are in English.</span></li>
