<h2 id="anchor-1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">1. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/google-ux-design-36437" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google UX Design (Google)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85706" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85706" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85706" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Google-UX-Design-Google.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Google-UX-Design-Google.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Google-UX-Design-Google-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Google-UX-Design-Google-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Google-UX-Design-Google-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85706" class="wp-caption-text">Emily, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My first pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/google-ux-design-36437" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google UX Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> professional certificate, offered by Google on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This professional certificate consists of the following 7 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-user-experience-design-35132" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Foundations of User Experience (UX) Design</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/start-ux-design-process-35137" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Start the UX Design Process: Empathize, Define, and Ideate</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/wireframes-low-fidelity-prototypes-35136" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Build Wireframes and Low-Fidelity Prototypes</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/conduct-ux-research-35135" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Conduct UX Research and Test Early Concepts</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/high-fidelity-designs-prototype-35134" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Create High-Fidelity Designs and Prototypes in Figma</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/responsive-web-design-adobe-xd-35133" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Responsive Web Design in Adobe XD</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-design-jobs-35131" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Design a User Experience for Social Good &amp; Prepare for Jobs</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this professional certificate, you’ll learn to create designs on paper and digital design tools like Figma and Adobe XD. You&#8217;ll gain in-demand skills and create three end-to-end projects that will make up your professional UX portfolio, so you&#8217;re ready to apply for jobs upon completion.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/foundations-user-experience-design-35132" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Foundations of User Experience (UX) Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn about UX fundamentals, job responsibilities of entry-level UX designers, career paths in UX, design sprints, and UX research methods while accounting for biases.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/start-ux-design-process-35137" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Start the UX Design Process: Empathize, Define, and Ideate</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn to empathize with users, create empathy maps, personas, user stories, and user journey maps, develop problem statements, generate ideas for solutions, conduct competitive audits, and design a mobile app, to add to your professional UX portfolio.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/wireframes-low-fidelity-prototypes-35136" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Build Wireframes and Low-Fidelity Prototypes</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn to develop a goal statement, create storyboards, wireframes and prototypes for a mobile app design, apply principles of information architecture and recognize implicit bias and deceptive patterns in design.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/conduct-ux-research-35135" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Conduct UX Research and Test Early Concepts</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn to plan and conduct UX research studies, respect privacy, take notes, analyze data, develop persuasive presentation skills, and modify designs based on research insights to improve your professional portfolio mobile app.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/high-fidelity-designs-prototype-35134" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Create High-Fidelity Designs and Prototypes in Figma</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll be able to design and build high-fidelity prototypes, apply design principles, create design systems, and collaborate with engineering teams to complete mobile app designs for your professional portfolio.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/responsive-web-design-adobe-xd-35133" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Responsive Web Design in Adobe XD</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you will learn how to create a responsive website using the UX design process, Adobe XD, and design systems. You will also learn to plan and conduct usability studies, iterate on designs, and add a new project to your portfolio. Optional lessons include creating a UX-focused resume and finding introductory-level jobs in UX.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-design-jobs-35131" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Design a User Experience for Social Good &amp; Prepare for Jobs</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you will be able to design for social good, create wireframes and prototypes, add a new design project to your portfolio, and interview for entry-level UX design jobs or freelance work.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The professional certificate is broken down into 7 courses. Each course involves about 20 to 70 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My second pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ui-ux-design-18899" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">UI / UX Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> specialization, offered by California Institute of the Arts on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization consists of the following 4 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/visual-elements-user-interface-design-12103" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visual Elements of User Interface Design</span></a></li>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/web-design-strategy-12097" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Web Design: Strategy and Information Architecture</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/web-design-wireframes-prototypes-12101" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Web Design: Wireframes to Prototypes</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You&#8217;ll learn all stages of the development process, from user research to wireframes, and apply best practices to create effective screen-based experiences. What’s more – by enrolling into this course, you’ll also be eligible for a one-month free trial of UX tools from Optimal Workshop.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/visual-elements-user-interface-design-12103" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Visual Elements of User Interface Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn to design clear, consistent and intuitive UI by learning to articulate meaning with color, type and imagery. The course focuses on individual elements and components of an interface designer&#8217;s skillset, and offers practical instruction for designing a static screen-based interface.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-design-fundamentals-12102" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design Fundamentals</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"><br />
</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn to describe and apply best practices in UX design and understand how UX design shapes audience experience of content, with an emphasis on a design-centric approach to UX/UI design with practical, skill-based instruction.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/web-design-strategy-12097" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Web Design: Strategy and Information Architecture</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn job descriptions within the industry and where UX and UI skills fit in, differences between native apps and websites, distinctions between agile and waterfall approaches, importance of user and site personas in web design, and user testing.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/web-design-wireframes-prototypes-12101" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Web Design: Wireframes to Prototypes</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn responsive web design and the challenges of designing for mobile devices, importance of a mobile-first approach, web typography, relationship between design and programming, and different web technologies like HTML, CSS, JavaScript, server-side coding and databases.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-3"><span style="font-weight: 400;">3. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/michiganux-18889" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience Research and Design (University of Michigan)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85708" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85708" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85708" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-User-Experience-Research-and-Design-University-of-Michigan.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-User-Experience-Research-and-Design-University-of-Michigan.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-User-Experience-Research-and-Design-University-of-Michigan-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-User-Experience-Research-and-Design-University-of-Michigan-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-User-Experience-Research-and-Design-University-of-Michigan-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85708" class="wp-caption-text">Clifford Lampe, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My third pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/michiganux-18889" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience Research and Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> specialization, offered by University of Michigan on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization consists of the following 6 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/introtoux-principles-and-processes-12348" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introduction to User Experience Principles and Processes</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/understanding-user-needs-12352" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Understanding User Needs</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/evaluating-designs-with-users-12357" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Evaluating Designs with Users</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-design-concept-wireframe-12350" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design: From Concept to Prototype</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-research-at-scale-12351" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Research at Scale: Surveys, Analytics, Online Testing</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-experience-capstone-12355" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX (User Experience) Capstone</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization will teach you how to understand user needs, rapidly generate prototypes, and evaluate design concepts while gaining hands-on experience taking a product from initial concept to user research, ideation, refinement, formal analysis, prototyping, and user testing.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/introtoux-principles-and-processes-12348" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introduction to User Experience Principles and Processes</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers UX research and design skills, including discovering user needs and conducting micro-usability tests. It teaches how to use sketching and prototyping to develop design concepts and incorporate a user-centered focus into the design process, and human behavior and techniques for designing interactive systems based on it.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/understanding-user-needs-12352" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Understanding User Needs</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches how to conduct qualitative research to understand user needs. It covers semi-structured interviews, in-situ observation, affinity walls, and how to conduct these research methods and gain experience using them.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/evaluating-designs-with-users-12357" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Evaluating Designs with Users</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn various user testing approaches and when to use them, designing effective user tests, running successful user tests, and analyzing and reporting user testing results.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-design-concept-wireframe-12350" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design: From Concept to Prototype</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches how to define the design problem, create user stories, sketch and brainstorm design ideas, develop wireframes and mockups, conduct user testing, and create prototypes for complex interactions and non-screen-based systems.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ux-research-at-scale-12351" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Research at Scale: Surveys, Analytics, Online Testing</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers web analytics and A/B testing, remote unmoderated testing, and analyzing large-scale user experience studies. You&#8217;ll learn about the different types and uses of surveys in UX research, including developing a survey instrument, analyzing and reporting on surveys, and critiquing user surveys.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-experience-capstone-12355" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX (User Experience) Capstone</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn how to design and execute a user experience research and design project. You will gain real-world experience by working on a realistic UX design project and learn how to effectively communicate your design concepts and research findings.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The specialization is broken down into 6 courses. Each course involves about 10 to 20 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">Fun Facts</span></h3>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Newman earned his Ph.D. and M.S. in Computer Science from UC Berkeley and his B.A. in Philosophy from Macalester College.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Klasnja received a Ph.D. in Information Science at the Information School at the University of Washington</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Hogan is a graduate of the University of Michigan (MSI), The University of Chicago (MLA), and the University of Pennsylvania (BA).</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Toyama graduated from Yale with a PhD in Computer Science and from Harvard with a bachelor’s degree in Physics.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Lampe received his PhD in Information in 2006 from the University of Michigan.</span></li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anchor-4"><span style="font-weight: 400;">4. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-ux-design-21087" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design (HEC Montréal)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85709" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85709" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85709" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-UX-Design-HEC-Montreal.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-UX-Design-HEC-Montreal.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-UX-Design-HEC-Montreal-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-UX-Design-HEC-Montreal-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-UX-Design-HEC-Montreal-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85709" class="wp-caption-text">Annemarie Lesage, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My fourth pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-ux-design-21087" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by HEC Montréal on edX.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Whether you’re making minor changes or major digital overhauls, you&#8217;ll also learn convergent ideation methods to anchor new concepts within your business context and seek win-win innovation for everyone involved. No prior knowledge is necessary in order to take this course.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn about the user-centered design approach and how to integrate UX research into the UX design process. You’ll explore the concepts of incremental, radical, and disruptive innovation, and how to apply design thinking theory and practice. Finally, you’ll understand divergent and convergent ideation methods, as well as how to analyze ideation results.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>

<h2 id="anchor-5"><span style="font-weight: 400;">5. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-design-18758" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Interaction Design (University of California, San Diego)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85710" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85710" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85710" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/5.-Interaction-Design-University-of-California-San-Diego.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/5.-Interaction-Design-University-of-California-San-Diego.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/5.-Interaction-Design-University-of-California-San-Diego-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/5.-Interaction-Design-University-of-California-San-Diego-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/5.-Interaction-Design-University-of-California-San-Diego-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85710" class="wp-caption-text">Elizabeth Gerber, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My fifth pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-design-18758" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Interaction Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> specialization, offered by University of California, San Diego on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization consists of the following 7 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/human-computer-interaction-4287" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Human-Centered Design: an Introduction</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/design-principles-4296" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Design Principles: an Introduction</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-techniques-4245" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Input and Interaction</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-research-2788" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience: Research &amp; Prototyping</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/infodesign-2787" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Information Design</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/designexperiments-2789" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Designing, Running, and Analyzing Experiments</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-design-capstone-5140" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Interaction Design Capstone Project</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll learn how to come up with design ideas and rapidly prototype them, using feedback from stakeholders like team members, clients and users. You&#8217;ll also explore principles of visual design, perception and cognition that are key to effective interaction design.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/human-computer-interaction-4287" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Human-Centered Design: an Introduction</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches you how to design enjoyable technologies and use techniques like rapid prototyping and comparative evaluation. You&#8217;ll learn to conduct fieldwork, make interactive paper prototypes and use them to gather feedback.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/design-principles-4296" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Design Principles: an Introduction</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers fundamental design principles, including visual design, interaction design, and perception and cognition. You will also learn how to evaluate your work with users through controlled online experiments.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-techniques-4245" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Input and Interaction</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course will teach you the fundamentals of human motor performance, perception, and cognition that inform effective interaction design. You’ll be able to design more effective input and interaction techniques for both traditional graphic and gestural interfaces.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-research-2788" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience: Research &amp; Prototyping</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers the core process of experience design and methods of design research to understand people and their context. You&#8217;ll learn to generate and refine ideas to create meaningful actionable insights and opportunities for design in different industries.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/infodesign-2787" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Information Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers visual design principles and concrete strategies for creating effective user interfaces, including typography, information architecture, layout, and color. It addresses specific design issues and how to apply design principles across diverse form factors.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/designexperiments-2789" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Designing, Running, and Analyzing Experiments</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches you how to design and analyze user-centered experiments to evaluate and validate user experiences. You&#8217;ll learn through real-world examples from UX, IxD, and HCI fields, and analyze data using the R programming language.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/interaction-design-capstone-5140" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Interaction Design Capstone Project</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll apply the skills learned from the course sequence to redesign a new interface, service, or product for your Interaction Design Capstone Project. You’ll develop real-world design challenges for this final project which can be shared in your design portfolio.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The specialization is broken down into 8 courses. Each course involves about 10 to 35 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-6"><span style="font-weight: 400;">6. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/extended-reality-for-everybody-23748" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Extended Reality for Everybody (University of Michigan)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85711" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85711" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85711" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/6.-Extended-Reality-for-Everybody-University-of-Michigan.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/6.-Extended-Reality-for-Everybody-University-of-Michigan.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/6.-Extended-Reality-for-Everybody-University-of-Michigan-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/6.-Extended-Reality-for-Everybody-University-of-Michigan-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/6.-Extended-Reality-for-Everybody-University-of-Michigan-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85711" class="wp-caption-text">Michael Nebeling, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My sixth pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/extended-reality-for-everybody-23748" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Extended Reality for Everybody</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> specialization, offered by University of Michigan on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization consists of the following 3 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/intro-augmented-virtual-mixed-extended-reality-te-23274" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Intro to AR/VR/MR/XR: Technologies, Applications &amp; Issues</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-experience-interaction-design-augmented-virt-23275" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience &amp; Interaction Design for AR/VR/MR/XR</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/develop-augmented-virtual-mixed-extended-reality--23273" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Developing AR/VR/MR/XR Apps with WebXR, Unity &amp; Unreal</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">These courses cover the basic concepts of XR, application development and design, emerging key issues in the XR landscape, and bringing XR into instructional settings. Whether you’re a beginner or an expert, this program is open to everyone, just as the name suggests.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/intro-augmented-virtual-mixed-extended-reality-te-23274" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Intro to AR/VR/MR/XR: Technologies, Applications &amp; Issues</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers the basics of XR (AR, VR, MR, and XR) and provides an overview of the XR landscape, including current and future devices and platforms. It also addresses social and ethical issues, accessibility, and security concerns in XR.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-experience-interaction-design-augmented-virt-23275" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience &amp; Interaction Design for AR/VR/MR/XR</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers the XR design process, design thinking, critiques, ethics, and user-centered techniques like design jams. The course also introduces various physical and digital prototyping methods and tools, including immersive authoring on XR devices.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/develop-augmented-virtual-mixed-extended-reality--23273" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Developing AR/VR/MR/XR Apps with WebXR, Unity &amp; Unreal</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course provides a broad overview of the XR landscape, design thinking principles, prototyping techniques, and development platforms and tools. You’ll gain a foundational understanding of XR technologies as well as the skills to create and evaluate XR applications.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The specialization is broken down into 3 courses. Each course involves about 28 to 33 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-7"><span style="font-weight: 400;">7. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-interface-design-32181" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Interface Design (University of Minnesota)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85712" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85712" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85712" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/7.-User-Interface-Design-Minnesota.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/7.-User-Interface-Design-Minnesota.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/7.-User-Interface-Design-Minnesota-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/7.-User-Interface-Design-Minnesota-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/7.-User-Interface-Design-Minnesota-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85712" class="wp-caption-text">Loren Terveen, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My seventh pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/user-interface-design-32181" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Interface Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> specialization, offered by University of Minnesota on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization consists of the following 4 courses:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ui-design-6890" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introduction to UI Design</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/design-research-6924" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Research and Design</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/prototyping-design-6932" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prototyping and Design</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ui-testing-6926" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Evaluating User Interfaces</span></a></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This specialization teaches you how to create successful user interfaces by covering user research, prototyping, and evaluation techniques. You’ll gain experience with structured approaches for understanding user needs, prototyping and design methods, and evaluation techniques to make informed design choices.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ui-design-6890" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Introduction to UI Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches the importance of user interface design and provides industry-standard methods for designing interfaces. You&#8217;ll learn about the design process for improving existing designs and starting new ones. The course also covers core UI design theories and concepts to avoid reinventing the wheel.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/design-research-6924" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Research and Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course covers user research and UI design exploration techniques. You&#8217;ll learn various research methods, analyze and deliver research findings, and practice ideation techniques to generate design ideas.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/prototyping-design-6932" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Prototyping and Design</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn and practice paper and low-fidelity prototyping techniques, apply graphic design principles and design patterns, write design rationales, and create accessible designs for specific populations and situations through lectures and exercises.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/ui-testing-6926" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Evaluating User Interfaces</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches techniques for evaluating user interfaces, including action analysis, heuristic evaluation, and user testing. It covers how to set and measure usability goals and determine when a design is ready for release.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The specialization is broken down into 4 courses. Each course involves about 10 to 15 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-8"><span style="font-weight: 400;">8. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-user-experience-for-web-design-100654" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience for Web Design (LinkedIn Learning)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85713" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85713" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85713" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/8.-User-Experience-for-Web-Design-LinkedIn-Learning.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/8.-User-Experience-for-Web-Design-LinkedIn-Learning.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/8.-User-Experience-for-Web-Design-LinkedIn-Learning-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/8.-User-Experience-for-Web-Design-LinkedIn-Learning-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/8.-User-Experience-for-Web-Design-LinkedIn-Learning-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85713" class="wp-caption-text">Chris Nodder, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My eighth pick for the best User Experience online course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-user-experience-for-web-design-100654" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">User Experience for Web Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on LinkedIn Learning.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Gain insights into creating interactive content and how to view your site from your users&#8217; perspective in order to better meet their needs. This course with a </span><b>1-month free trial</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> will teach you how people search for information online, how to structure your content, and how to use graphics and media effectively.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn how to create a good web user experience by defining your visitors, focusing on information, and designing simple and consistent pages. You&#8217;ll also learn how to create good content that determines your design, how people read on the web, formatting for information exchange and using media.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">After that, you&#8217;ll understand how to balance adverts and content, choose menu placement, create mobile menus, provide good information scent, use Fitts&#8217; law, and create landing pages from ad campaigns, create detailed and product pages, handle errors in forms, and apply good design practice.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 11 modules. Each module involves about 10 to 20 minutes of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos and quizzes.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-9"><span style="font-weight: 400;">9. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/principles-of-ux-ui-design-108437" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Principles of UI/UX Design (Meta)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85714" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85714" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85714" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/9.-UX-Design-Meta.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/9.-UX-Design-Meta.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/9.-UX-Design-Meta-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/9.-UX-Design-Meta-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/9.-UX-Design-Meta-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85714" class="wp-caption-text">Instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My ninth pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/principles-of-ux-ui-design-108437" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Principles of UI/UX Design</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by Meta on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course teaches you the basics of UX research and design, including how to identify problems, empathize with users, and create user personas. You&#8217;ll also learn the UI design process and how to create wireframes and MVP prototypes using Figma, as well as the key design principles.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn the fundamentals of UX and UI design and what constitutes a successful UI. You’ll understand how to evaluate and improve interactive design using best practices and develop your UI design by creating, sharing, and testing it. The course ends with a summary of the skills learned and a final assessment.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 5 modules. Each module involves about 4 to 6 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<h2 id="anchor-10"><span style="font-weight: 400;">10. </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udacity-ux-design-for-mobile-developers-2212" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design for Mobile Developers (Google)</span></a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85715" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85715" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85715" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/10.-UX-Design-for-Mobile-Developers-Google.png" alt="" width="1537" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/10.-UX-Design-for-Mobile-Developers-Google.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/10.-UX-Design-for-Mobile-Developers-Google-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/10.-UX-Design-for-Mobile-Developers-Google-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/10.-UX-Design-for-Mobile-Developers-Google-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85715" class="wp-caption-text">Izabel (left) and Nazmul (right), instructors</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My tenth pick for the best User Experience online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/udacity-ux-design-for-mobile-developers-2212" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">UX Design for Mobile Developers</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by Google on Udacity.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is a good option for developers who want to quickly improve their UX design skills in a mobile/Android context. By focusing on important design techniques, the course aims to teach developers how to plan and prototype effective apps before writing any code.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">What You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you&#8217;ll learn about User Experience (UX) and how it differs from User Interface (UI), as well as the importance of high-level planning and low-fi wireframing and prototyping. The course also covers User-Centered Design and how to create effective personas and use cases using low-cost user research.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You&#8217;ll also learn about designing for mobile constraints, including limited data, finite battery, hand-held usage, divided user attention, and small screens. The course concludes with designing for Android delight, including Android sensors, contextual apps and Android APIs such as Google Play Services.</span></p>
<h3><span style="font-weight: 400;">How You’ll Learn</span></h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 4 lessons and involves about 4 weeks of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos and quizzes.</span></p>

		<title>Learning with MOOCs 2023: Abstracts Due April 3rd</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/learning-with-moocs-2023/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/learning-with-moocs-2023/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Manoel Cortes Mendez]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Tue, 14 Mar 2023 14:04:57 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[News]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Conferences]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=85718</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>The conference hosted by MIT welcomes submissions on MOOCs, blended learning, and open education.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/learning-with-moocs-2023/">Learning with MOOCs 2023: Abstracts Due April 3rd</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/lwmoocs-2023-banner.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85720" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/lwmoocs-2023-banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/lwmoocs-2023-banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/lwmoocs-2023-banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/lwmoocs-2023-banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<p>This year, the IEEE conference <a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/">Learning with MOOCs</a> (LWMOOCs) will be hosted at MIT in Cambridge, Massachusetts, USA, on October 11–13. This marks a return to origins for the event: its first edition took place at MIT, back in 2014.</p>
<p>The conference, which primarily focuses on massive open online courses, welcomes submissions from a broad range of participants, including researchers, educators, decision-makers, and practitioners.</p>
<p>In 2023, besides its usual themes centered around MOOCs, the event is formally broadening its scope to encompass blended learning and open education at large. Furthermore, this edition is particularly interested in contributions that seek to refine the notion of &#8220;success&#8221; within the context of open-education projects.</p>
<p><a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/registration-information">Registrations</a> will open soon; the <a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/authors/call-for-papers">call for papers is already available here</a>. The deadline for submitting an abstract is <strong>April 3rd</strong>, while full papers are due a month later. Get your submissions ready!</p>
<h2>Conference Program</h2>
<p>Since the conference is half a year away, the detailed conference program and speaker list haven&#8217;t been released yet. But having taken part in several past editions, the event usually features a balance of short- and long-form talks from experts. This edition will be no exception. The three-day program will include:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Keynotes</strong>, by leading experts — the occasion for deep dives into specific topics.</li>
<li><strong>Full paper presentations</strong>, exploring at length comprehensive submissions.</li>
<li><strong>Lightning rounds</strong>, with authors taking turns, concisely presenting their work.</li>
<li><strong>Workshops</strong>, taking a hands-on, interactive approach to the subject at hand.</li>
<li><strong>Poster sessions</strong>, facilitating one-on-one discussion with paper authors.</li>
</ul>
<p>In addition, you can expect the conference to offer optional social activities — opportunities for networking, collaboration, less formal communication, and perhaps, for discovering the city of Cambridge and all it has to offer.</p>
<p>You can find more details on the <a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/">conference program here</a>.</p>
<h2>Call for Papers</h2>
<p>The conference welcomes submissions on a wide variety of topics pertaining to MOOCs — spanning MOOC development, delivery, and analytics — as well as blended learning, and open education initiatives.</p>
<p>Specific topics of interest include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Free or affordable degrees, including MOOC-based programs</li>
<li>The role and potential of MOOCs in the professional world</li>
<li>Inclusivity and accessibility in open education</li>
<li>International cooperation in MOOC projects</li>
<li>Machine learning and AI in online learning</li>
<li>Course and curriculum design</li>
<li>Learning analytics</li>
</ul>
<p>You can find a more complete list of <a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/">example topics here</a>.</p>
<p>Submissions will undergo a two-step, double-blind review process. A structured abstract (up to 2 pages) will be submitted first. Upon acceptance, authors will submit their full paper (up to 6 pages) for second review and full acceptance.</p>
<p>The first deadline is fast approaching. Here&#8217;s the submission process timeline:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>April 3</strong>: Abstract upload deadline.</li>
<li><strong>April 14</strong>: Abstract acceptance notification.</li>
<li><strong>May 12</strong>: Full paper upload deadline.</li>
<li><strong>June 30</strong>: Full paper acceptance notification.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Registration</h2>
<p>If you&#8217;d like to attend the conference, you can find the <a href="https://2023.lwmoocs-conference.org/registration-information">registration page here</a>. Registrations haven&#8217;t opened yet, but you&#8217;ll find information there regarding registration fees, including the early bird rates.</p>
<p><i>Class Central is a media partner of LWMOOCs 2023.</i></p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/learning-with-moocs-2023/">Learning with MOOCs 2023: Abstracts Due April 3rd</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>

										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85690" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-BCG-Banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-BCG-Banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-BCG-Banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-BCG-Banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Crystal is an object-oriented programming language that combines the speed and power of C with the expressiveness and readability of Ruby, making it easy to write and easy to understand.</p>
<p>With Crystal, you can write less code and get more done. With a built-in type inference system that eliminates the need for explicit type annotations, if your code compiles, your code is guaranteed to be type error-free at compile time.</p>
<p>But don&#8217;t let its ease of use and high levels of abstraction fool you into thinking that it’ll be sluggish — nay, Crystal is extremely fast! It is built on top of the LLVM compiler infrastructure, giving it performance on par with C and C++. This means that your Crystal code can run faster and use less memory than code written in other languages.</p>
<p>Not only is Crystal a great choice for building web applications and servers, thanks to its growing ecosystem of community libraries and frameworks such as <a href="https://amberframework.org/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Amber</a> that replaces <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-ruby-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ruby on Rails</a> or <a href="https://kemalcr.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Kemal</a> that replaces Sinatra, you can go even beyond.</p>
<p>Are you ready to dive into the world of Crystal programming? Read on to see my top picks for the best course to learn Crystal.</p>

<h2>What is Crystal?</h2>
<p>Crystal is a general-purpose, object-oriented programming language designed for high performance and readability. Developed in 2014 by Ary Borenszweig, Juan Wajnerman, Brian Cardiff, and a team of over 300 contributors, Crystal has a seductive tagline: “<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8FvrBLWUwxc" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Fast as C, slick as Ruby</a>”.</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Fast as C: </b><a href="https://digitalcollection.zhaw.ch/bitstream/11475/22807/4/2021_Ganz-Spielberger_Performance-evaluation-of-Crystal.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal is about 10% slower than C</a>. This is quite impressive considering that C is a low-level language with no garbage collection while Crystal is a high-level language with garbage collection. In comparison, Ruby is about 8 times slower than Crystal. Crystal’s blazingly fast performance can be attributed to its LLVM compiler infrastructure, the same compiler technology used by C and C++ itself, as well as other famously fast languages such as Fortran, Rust, and Julia. Crystal also prides itself on its C interoperability, making it easy to call native C libraries. And if you want to see how Crystal fares in real-world usage, just compare the <a href="https://kemalcr.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Kemal</a> framework (Crystal) to Sinatra (Ruby) and Ruby on Rails (Ruby) in the barchart below.</li>
</ul>
<figure id="attachment_85691" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85691" style="width: 705px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85691" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-Chart-Speed.png" alt="" width="705" height="436" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-Chart-Speed.png 705w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Crystal-Chart-Speed-300x186.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 705px) 100vw, 705px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85691" class="wp-caption-text">Chart created by Dmitry Rocha, from <a href="https://blog.codeminer42.com/crystal-by-numbers-8a675b0572fc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal by Numbers Benchmarking Kemal, Ruby on Rails, and Sinatra | The Miners</a></figcaption></figure>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Slick as Ruby:</b> Crystal’s syntax is heavily inspired by Ruby — if you’re a Ruby veteran, you’ll feel right at home. But if you have not touched Ruby in your life, you’ll still find yourself picking up the language quite fast due to its simple, human-readable syntax. Additionally, Crystal has a built-in package manager called Shards (similar to Ruby’s gems) which makes it easy to install and manage dependencies.</li>
</ul>
<p>But unlike Ruby, Crystal is statically type-checked, which means type errors will be caught early by the compiler rather than fail on runtime. Don’t worry though, you don’t need to explicitly define types as the compiler can intelligently infer types. Crystal also supports many modern features such as a macro system for powerful metaprogramming capabilities as well as support for concurrency, making it well-suited for high-performance and concurrent systems.</p>
<p>Crystal has a wide range of applications, including web development, systems programming, and data processing. It is often <a href="https://crystal-lang.org/used_in_prod/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">used by companies</a> such as <a href="https://www.84codes.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">84codes</a>, <a href="https://invidious.io/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Invidious</a>, and <a href="https://www.protel.com.tr/en/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Protel</a> for building web servers, web APIs, and web scraping tools, due to its performance and expressiveness. And since it is concurrent, Crystal is also suitable for building command-line tools, distributed systems, and data processing pipelines. Though Crystal is relatively niche even compared to other niche languages out there, Crystal programmers are one of the most highly paid developers according to the <a href="https://survey.stackoverflow.co/2022/#section-top-paying-technologies-top-paying-technologies" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2022 Stack Overflow Developer survey</a>, with a median yearly salary of $84,690.</p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2>
<p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">100K online courses</a> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/crystal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal courses</a> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener">learner</a>.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, affordability, release date, ratings and enrollments.</li>
</ol>
<h2>Course Ranking Statistics</h2>
<p>Here are some aggregate stats about the ranking:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">All of the courses are suitable for beginners to Crystal, while two courses are friendly towards complete newbies to programming.</li>
<li aria-level="1">All of the courses require you to run MacOs, Linux, or if you’re on Windows, WSL2. This is because Crystal is not yet fully supported on Windows at the time of writing.</li>
<li aria-level="1">All of the courses except for two are <b>free</b>.</li>
</ul>
<p>Without further ado, let’s go through the top picks.</p>
<h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-know-ruby-enter-crystal-125886" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal For Rubyists (Serdar Dogruyol)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85683" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Crystal-For-Rubyists-Serdar-Dogruyol.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Crystal-For-Rubyists-Serdar-Dogruyol.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Crystal-For-Rubyists-Serdar-Dogruyol-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/1.-Crystal-For-Rubyists-Serdar-Dogruyol-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My number one pick for the best Crystal course is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-know-ruby-enter-crystal-125886" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal For Rubyists</a> written by Serdar Dogruyol.</p>
<p>This short yet comprehensive guide that aims to help developers learn and understand the Crystal programming language by contrasting Ruby with Crystal. Though the course name may sound like it&#8217;s only aimed towards Ruby developers, it actually means that it assumes no knowledge of types, pointers, concurrency, or other similar things. Non-ruby developers are welcomed!</p>
<p>You’ll cover the basics of writing your first Crystal program, types, concurrency, metaprogramming, and more. By the end, you’ll have enough knowledge of Crystal to start exploring Crystal’s frameworks and libraries.</p>
<p>Prior experience with programming is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>After understanding the advantages of Crystal over Ruby and installing Crystal on your PC, you’ll get right into writing your first Crystal program. You’ll learn the basics of a Crystal project — implementing FizzBuzz in the language — which will help you grasp Crystal’s syntax and structure, as well as learn how to run Crystal programs.</p>
<p>Rubyists love testing. You’ll quickly discover that Crystal makes it easy to write and run tests using its built-in framework.</p>
<p>Rubyists love dynamic typing; Crystal is statically typed. Though most of the time. Crystal doesn’t feel like it&#8217;s statically typed anyways because you rarely need to specify the type thanks to intelligent type inference. And because of static types, you’ll find out about method overloading, where you have different methods with the same name and different number of arguments.</p>
<p>Crystal offers first-class support for concurrent programming through Channels. You’ll learn how to spawn multiple messages at the same time. You&#8217;ll also discover how Crystal&#8217;s metaprogramming capabilities can rival those of Ruby (even though Ruby is interpreted whereas Crystal is compiled), along with how to interoperate with C libraries using C bindings. Because why write something that has already been written?</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course consists of 10 chapters. You’ll learn by reading through the course chapters and looking at the code examples provided.</p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Serdar Dogruyol is the author of <a href="https://kemalcr.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Kemal</a> (the blazingly fast web framework you saw in <a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1cPBVvPzcPQSX3ltGAns-MzU5YIc9lom_uKk_D0ZW8xc/edit#heading=h.3jb59mwxxg6f" target="_blank" rel="noopener">What is Crystal?</a>), a curator of Crystal Weekly, and a Crystal Core Member. He’s a Crystalian who has extensive experience working with a variety of languages, including Ruby, Java, PHP, Crystal, and Elixir.</li>
<li aria-level="1">As this course does not provide any exercises, you should try doing some which are offered in the 6th and 7th ranking of this article.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anchor-2">2. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-crystal-language-125885" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tutorials &#8211; Crystal (crystal-lang.org)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85684" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/2.-Tutorials-Crystal-crystal-lang.org_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/2.-Tutorials-Crystal-crystal-lang.org_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/2.-Tutorials-Crystal-crystal-lang.org_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/2.-Tutorials-Crystal-crystal-lang.org_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My second pick for the best Crystal course are <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-crystal-language-125885" target="_blank" rel="noopener">the open-source tutorials hosted on the official Crystal language website</a>.</p>
<p>Targeted at novice Crystal programmers and people with no experience with programming, you’ll learn the basics of the Crystal language in a very short amount of time.</p>
<p>The content is sufficient but limited. I recommend that you supplement your learning with the 6th and 7th practical courses in this ranking.</p>
<p>Prior programming experience is recommended, but not required.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll begin this course with the famous first message every programmer has ingrained into their brains — ”Hello World!”. Although it&#8217;s simple, you’ll get to know the structure of a Crystal program this way, that is top-level scope is treated as part of the main program.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll learn about variables and data types. One thing to note is that variables can be reassigned to different values and even different data types, which may feel a lot like dynamic types in <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-ruby-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ruby</a>. Then, you’ll also learn how to do arithmetic and string operations in Crystal, which are very much painless to perform.</p>
<p>Every programming language needs to have control constructs as well as methods. You’ll learn how to use conditionals and loops to have your program make or repeat decisions. Methods, on the other hand, allow you to avoid duplicating the same chunk of code. You’ll learn how to create methods with arguments and type restrictions to ensure correctness of your program.</p>
<p>Finally, you’ll be given two examples of simple programs for you to explore. One of them is a command line application where you’ll learn how to deal with getting user input and producing an output, whereas the other will open your eyes to server processing with HTTP servers.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is made up of multiple tutorials focusing on different aspects of the language. You’ll learn by reading through them as well as by studying the example applications provided.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-3">3. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-crystal-course-125880" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal Course (Groxio)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85685" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-Crystal-Course-Groxio.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-Crystal-Course-Groxio.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-Crystal-Course-Groxio-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/3.-Crystal-Course-Groxio-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My third pick for the best course is a bit peculiar.</p>
<p>Groxio’s <b>paid</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-crystal-course-125880" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Crystal Course</a> combines a course book, videos (informational and instructional), community resources, and coding projects all in one package.</p>
<p>By following the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dreyfus_model_of_skill_acquisition" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Dreyfus learning model</a>, Groxio provides the necessary step-by-step instructions for beginners to start Crystal, and perhaps more crucially, exercises and projects that intermediates need to follow up with in order to break from their newbie status.</p>
<p>If you’re willing to shell out a little bit of cash for a multimodal learning experience, this course wouldn’t disappoint!</p>
<p>You should have some experience with programming prior to taking this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll begin with an elucidation of the fundamental principles and philosophy behind Crystal to help you appreciate the language. Afterward, you’ll engross yourself in the basic details of Crystal, such as installation and syntax. By creating a simple “Hello, World!” program, you’ll help crystallize the structure of a typical project into your mindspace, before diving deeper in the details.</p>
<p>Next, you&#8217;ll explore decision-making with cases and if statements, and learn how to group and manipulate data with arrays, tuples, and hashes. You&#8217;ll also discover the power of procs and blocks for creating reusable code.</p>
<p>Moving on, you’ll get a test of the object-oriented side of Crystal with classes and modules. You&#8217;ll learn how to organize and structure code in larger projects, and grasp key OOP concepts like instantiation, inheritance, and polymorphism. These concepts will help you write complex and scalable software, making it easier to maintain and upgrade in the future.</p>
<p>Crystal is a statically typed language. You’ll learn and master types by first understanding their importance — to ensure code correctness at compile time. You’ll also learn how to create and wield your own custom types to protect your code from potential errors too. Finally, you’ll bring everything together by planning, building, and deploying Crystal projects, including managing dependencies and concurrency, through actual hands-on projects.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course consists of a course book, video tutorials, community resources, and projects. You’ll learn by reading through the book chapters, watching videos about the Crystal language as well as videos by the instructor where they code hands-on, checking out the handy community resources, and most importantly, working on the larger coding projects.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-4">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-crystal-125879" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn Programming in Crystal Lang course (Gábor Szabó)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85686" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-Learn-Programming-in-Crystal-Lang-course-Gabor-Szabo.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-Learn-Programming-in-Crystal-Lang-course-Gabor-Szabo.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-Learn-Programming-in-Crystal-Lang-course-Gabor-Szabo-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/4.-Learn-Programming-in-Crystal-Lang-course-Gabor-Szabo-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Gábor Szabó has <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-crystal-125879" target="_blank" rel="noopener">an excellent introductory course to Crystal programming</a>.</p>
<p>I like this <b>free</b> course particularly because it’s easy to let the video play, sitback, and learn. This is because Gábor Szabó is an excellent teacher who can explain in detail what is happening on screen with his <a href="https://code-maven.com/slides/crystal/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">well-crafted slides and examples</a>. Though of course, it’d be a much more effective learning experience if you were to follow along writing down code examples at home.</p>
<p>The video series covers most but not all of the slides in the link, so by the end of the course, you’ll have learned the basics of the Crystal language, including its syntax, type system, and how to run code. You should check out the slides, as they also give you exercises to try and complete.</p>
<p>If you have an hour to spare to see what Crystal is all about, and also have some prior programming experience, this is a great course for you.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>In this course, you&#8217;ll learn the basics of the Crystal language. After some brief set up (running Crystal in a Docker container and exploring third party libraries called ‘shards’), you’ll begin learning how variables and data types work in Crystal. Indeed, you’ll be amazed by Crystal’s static but versatile types, from primitive to compound types, and concatenating strings to doing mathematical operations on numbers. You’ll be able to write a command line program that takes arguments passed into the standard input (STDIN) and prints a result to the screen.</p>
<p>You’ll also learn about early exit in Crystal, create basic shapes like rectangles, discover the concept of interactive environments, and also how to write Crystal one-liners. Last but not least, you’ll learn how to generate random numbers in Crystal.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 3–4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the videos in the series and following along with the instructor. Additionally, you can complete the exercises given to strengthen your understanding of the Crystal programming concepts.</p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>

<li aria-level="1">He also has other courses written for beginners such as a <b>free </b><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-perl-tutorial-119192" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Perl tutorial</a> as well as a <a href="https://courses.code-maven.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Perl, Python, and Go courses bundle</a>.</li>
</ul>
